# <a name="essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="9765f-103">Osnovne usluge za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-103">Essential services for Office</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-104">Informacije u ovom članku se odnose na verziju 1904 ili noviju, sledećih Office klijentskih softvera instaliranih na računaru sa operativnim sistemom Windows:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-104">The information in this article applies to Version 1904 or later of the following Office client software installed on a computer running Windows:</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-105">Office 365 ProPlus i Office 365 Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-105">Office 365 ProPlus and Office 365 Business</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home ili druge verzije sistema Office koje su deo pretplate na Office 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-106">Office 365 Personal, Office 365 Home, or other versions of Office that are part of an Office 365 subscription.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-107">Project i Visio koji se dobijaju uz neke planove pretplata, kao što je plan za Project Online Professional ili Visio Online Plan 2.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-107">Project and Visio that come with some subscription plans, such as the Project Online Professional plan or Visio Online Plan 2.</span></span>


<span data-ttu-id="9765f-108">Office se sastoji od aplikacija klijentskog softvera i povezanih iskustava dizajniranih tako da vam omogućavaju da efikasnije kreirate, komunicirate i sarađujete.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-108">Office consists of client software applications and connected experiences designed to enable you to create, communicate, and collaborate more effectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-109">Iako možete da kontrolišete mnoga povezana iskustva koja su dostupna vama ili, ako ste administrator organizacije, vašim korisnicima, postoji i skup usluga koje su od suštinske važnosti za funkcionisanje sistema Office, te stoga ne mogu biti onemogućene.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-109">While you can control many of the connected experiences that are available to you, or to your users if you’re the admin in your organization, there are a set of services that are essential to how Office functions and therefore cannot be disabled.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-110">Na primer, usluga licenciranja koja potvrđuje da ste ispravno licencirani da koristite Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-110">For example, the licensing service that confirms that you are properly licensed to use Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-111">Neophodni podaci o ovim uslugama prikupljaju se i šalju korporaciji Microsoft, bez obzira na bilo koje druge postavke smernica za privatnost koje ste konfigurisali.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-111">Required service data about these services is collected and sent to Microsoft, regardless of any other privacy-related policy settings that you have configured.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-112">Možete da vidite ove podatke tako što ćete koristiti Prikazivač dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-112">You can see this data by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-113">Dodatne informacije potražite u sledećim člancima:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-113">For more information, see the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-114">Neophodni podaci o usluzi za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-114">Required service data for Office</span></span>](required-service-data.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-115">Korišćenje Prikazivača dijagnostičkih podataka uz Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-115">Using the Diagnostic Data Viewer with Office</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/cf761ce9-d805-4c60-a339-4e07f3182855)
- [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-116">Povezana iskustva u sistemu Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-116">Connected experiences in Office</span></span>](connected-experiences.md)

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-117">Ako ste administrator organizacije, možda će vas zanimati i sledeće:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-117">If you’re the admin for your organization, you might also be interested in the following:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-118">Pregled kontrola privatnosti za Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-118">Overview of privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](overview-privacy-controls.md)
- [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-119">Korišćenje regulatornih postavki za upravljanje kontrolama privatnosti u programu Office 365 ProPlus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-119">Use policy settings to manage privacy controls for Office 365 ProPlus</span></span>](manage-privacy-controls.md)

## <a name="list-of-essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="9765f-120">Lista osnovnih usluga za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-120">List of essential services for Office</span></span> 

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-121">Sledeća tabela sadrži listu osnovnih usluga za Office i njihov opis.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-121">The following table provides a list of the essential services for Office and a description of each service.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="9765f-122">**Usluga**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-122">**Service**</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="9765f-123">**Opis**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-123">**Description**</span></span>  |
| ------ | ---- |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-124">Potvrda identiteta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-124">Authentication</span></span>](#authentication-events) | <span data-ttu-id="9765f-125">Potvrda identiteta je usluga koja se nalazi na bilo kom uređaju i koja potvrđuje vaš korisnički identitet u sistemu Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-125">Authentication is a cross-platform service that validates your Office user identity.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-126">Ona je potrebna za prijavljivanje u Office, aktiviranje Office licence, pristup vašim datotekama koje su uskladištene u oblaku i za pružanje doslednog iskustva u svim Office sesijama i uređajima.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-126"> It is required to enable you to sign in to Office, activate your Office license, access your files stored in the cloud, and provides a consistent experience across Office sessions and your devices.</span></span>    |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-127">Klikni i pokreni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-127">Click-to-Run</span></span>](#click-to-run-events) | <span data-ttu-id="9765f-128">„Klikni i pokreni“ je tehnologija instaliranja koja se koristi za instalaciju i ažuriranje sistema Office na operativnom sistemu Windows.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-128">Click-to-Run is the installation technology used to install and update Office on Windows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-129">Ona proverava da li postoje nove verzije sistema Office, a kada nova verzija postane dostupna, preuzima je i instalira.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-129">It checks for new versions of Office, and when a new version is available, downloads and installs it.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="9765f-130"> „Klikni i pokreni“ će otkrivati potrebu za preuzimanjem i instaliranjem Office ispravki, kao i bezbednosnih zakrpi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-130"> Click-to-Run will detect the need for, perform the download of, and install Office updates, including security updates.</span></span>     |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-131">Usluga poboljšane konfiguracije (UPK)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-131">Enhanced Configuration Service (ECS)</span></span>](#experimentation-and-configuration-service-ecs-events) | <span data-ttu-id="9765f-132">UPK omogućava korporaciji Microsoft da ponovo konfiguriše instalacije sistema Office, a da vi ne morate ponovo da ga instalirate.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-132">ECS provides Microsoft the ability to reconfigure Office installations without the need for you to redeploy Office.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-133">Koristi se za kontrolu postepenog objavljivanja funkcija i ažuriranja, dok se uticaj objavljivanja nadgleda preko dijagnostičkih podataka koji se prikupljaju.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-133">It is used to control the gradual rollout of features or updates, while the impact of the rollout is monitored from diagnostic data being collected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-134">Takođe se koristi i za smanjivanje bezbednosnih problema i problema performansi uz pomoć funkcija ili ažuriranja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-134">It is also used to mitigate security or performance issues with a feature or update.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-135">Osim toga, UPK podržava promene u konfiguraciji koje se odnose na dijagnostičke podatke kako bi se obezbedilo prikupljanje odgovarajućih događaja.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-135">In addition, ECS supports configuration changes related to diagnostic data to help ensure that the appropriate events are being collected.</span></span> |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-136">Licenciranje</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-136">Licensing</span></span>](#licensing-events)     | <span data-ttu-id="9765f-137">Licenciranje je usluga zasnovana na tehnologiji oblaka koja održava vašu Office aktivaciju tokom novih instalacija i čuva licencu na vašim uređajima nakon aktivacije.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-137">Licensing is a cloud-based service that supports your Office activation for new installations and maintains the license on your devices after Office has been activated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-138">Ona registruje svaki od vaših uređaja i aktivira Office, provera status vaše pretplate na sistem Office i upravlja vašom šifrom proizvoda.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-138">It registers each of your devices and activates Office, checks the status of your Office subscription, and manages your product keys.</span></span>    |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-139">Konfiguracija usluga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-139">Services Configuration</span></span>](#services-configuration-events)  | <span data-ttu-id="9765f-140">Konfiguracija usluga pruža mogućnost ažuriranja postavki konfiguracije za Office da bi se omogućile ili onemogućile funkcije klijenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-140">Services Configuration provides the ability to make updates to Office configuration settings to enable or disable client features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-141">Ova funkcija se poziva svaki put kada se pokrene Office aplikacija i pruža detalje o ostalim konfiguracijama i uslugama sistema Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-141">It is called every time an Office application is started and provides details about other Office configurations and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-142">Konfiguracija usluga takođe kontroliše koje usluge su određene kao osnovne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-142">Services Configuration also controls which services are designated as essential services.</span></span>  |
| [<span data-ttu-id="9765f-143">Telemetrija </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-143">Telemetry </span></span>](#telemetry-events)  | <span data-ttu-id="9765f-144">Usluga telemetrije se koristi za prikupljanje dijagnostičkih podataka iz Office aplikacija.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-144">The Telemetry service is used to collect diagnostic data from Office applications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-145">Ona omogućava prikupljanje dijagnostičkih podataka koje generiše Office, i obaveznih i opcionalnih.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-145">It enables the collection of the diagnostic data generated by Office, both required and optional diagnostic data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-146">Takođe je odgovorna za delimično prikupljanje neophodnih dijagnostičkih podataka o usluzi za Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-146">It is also responsible for the collection of the service diagnostic data portion of required service data for Office.</span></span>  |

## <a name="events-and-data-fields-for-essential-services-for-office"></a><span data-ttu-id="9765f-147">Događaji i polja sa podacima za osnovne usluge za Office</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-147">Events and data fields for essential services for Office</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-148">Odeljci u nastavku pružaju sledeće informacije:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-148">The next sections provide the following information:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9765f-149">Listu događaja za svaku osnovnu uslugu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-149">A list of events for each essential service</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9765f-150">Opis svakog događaja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-150">A description of each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9765f-151">Listu polja sa podacima u svakom događaju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-151">A list of data fields in each event</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9765f-152">Opis svakog polja sa podacima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-152">A description of each data field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-153">Možete da vidite ove događaje tako što ćete koristiti Prikazivač dijagnostičkih podataka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-153">You can see these events by using the Diagnostic Data Viewer.</span></span>



## <a name="authentication-events"></a><span data-ttu-id="9765f-154">Događaji potvrde identiteta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-154">Authentication events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-155">Ovi događaji dijagnostičkih podataka se prikupljaju kada Office pokuša da preuzme token potvrde identiteta, ili tiho ili putem upita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-155">These diagnostic data events are collected when Office attempts to acquire an authentication token, either silently or through prompting.</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentityfbapromptwin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="9765f-156">Office.Identity.FbaPromptWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-156">Office.Identity.FbaPromptWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-157">Prikuplja se kada Office prikaže korisniku Forms-Based-Auth upit za prijavljivanje zasnovan na formularu za potvrdu identiteta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-157">Collected when Office shows the user a Forms-Based-Auth sign-in prompt.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-158">Pored tihog preuzimanja tokena, upit za potvrdu identiteta se koristi da se odredi da li se korisnik nalazi u statusu neispravne potvrde identiteta, što bi za korisnika značilo da je stanje klijenta van mreže, a u najgorem slučaju, neispravna potvrda identiteta može sprečiti preuzimanje licence i dovesti do potpuno neupotrebljivog klijenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-158">Along with silent token acquisitions, authentication prompts is used to determine if user is in a broken authentication state which, for the user, results in what is essentially an Offline Client state, or in the worst case, broken authentication may prevent license acquisition and result in a completely unusable client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-159">Upiti za prijavljivanje zasnovani na formularu za potvrdu identiteta (FBA - Forms-Based-Auth) se koriste u nekim scenarijima za lokalnu potvrdu identiteta i uglavnom se trudimo da se to ne dešava jer bi svi trebalo da koriste modernu identifikaciju (modern-Auth) zbog bezbednosnih ranjivosti koje se odnose na FBA.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-159">Forms-Based-Auth (FBA) sign-in prompts are used for some on-premises authentication scenarios and typically we want to make sure this isn’t happening, as everyone should be using Modern-Auth because of security vulnerabilities associated with FBA.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-160">**Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-160">**The following fields are collected:**</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-161">**AuthScheme** - šema koja se koristi za potvrdu identiteta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-161">**AuthScheme** - the authentication scheme used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-162">**DocumentUrlHash** - šifrovani URL zahtevi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-162">**DocumentUrlHash** - an encrypted URL requesting</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-163">**EndTag** - oznaka gde je završen FBA obrazac</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-163">**EndTag** - the tag where FBA form is completed</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-164">**Flags** - zastarelo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-164">**Flags** - Obsolete</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-165">**EndTag** - oznaka gde počinje FBA obrazac</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-165">**FlowTag** - the tag where FBA form is started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-166">**LastError** - vraćanje koda greške</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-166">**LastError** – the error code returned</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-167">**PromptEndTime** - vreme kada je upit završen</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-167">**PromptEndTime** - the time when then prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-168">**PromptStartTime** - vreme kada je upit započet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-168">**PromptStartTime** - the time when the prompt started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-169">**Rezultat** - da li je potvrda identiteta uspela</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-169">**Result** - whether the authentication succeeded</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-170">**SessionEndTime** - vreme kada je sesija događaja završena</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-170">**SessionEndTime** – the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-171">**Timeout** - vreme kada je upit istekao</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-171">**Timeout** - the time when the prompt timed out</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentitysignoutevent"></a><span data-ttu-id="9765f-172">Office.Identity.SignOutEvent</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-172">Office.Identity.SignOutEvent</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-173">Prikuplja se kada se korisnik odjavi sa sistema Office.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-173">Collected when a user signs out of Office.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-174">Saznanje da se korisnik odjavio omogućava klasifikaciju ostalih događaja, kao što su upiti, na način na koji se očekuje kako bi se pravilno izračunala njihova pouzdanost / metrička spremnost otpreme i da bi se izbeglo upozorenje i vraćanje na prethodne verzije zasnovano na lažnoj premisi da korisnik ima neočekivane probleme sa upitima za potvrdu identiteta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-174">Knowing the user is signed-out makes it possible to classify other events, such as prompts, as expected, so those events can be correctly computed in reliability / ship-readiness metrics and avoid alerting or rolling back builds on the faulty premise that the user is experiencing unexpected sign-in prompts.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-175">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-175">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-176">**FlowEndTime** - vreme kada je aktivnost odjave završena</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-176">**FlowEndTime** - the time when the sign out action ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-177">**FlowEndTime** - vreme kada je aktivnost odjave započeta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-177">**FlowStartTime** - the time when the sign out action started</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-178">**IdentityErrorState** - bilo koji status greške identiteta prilikom odjave</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-178">**IdentityErrorState** - any identity error state during sign out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-179">**IdentityHashedUniqueId** - odjava šifrovanog ID identiteta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-179">**IdentityHashedUniqueId** - the encrypted identity ID being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-180">**IdentityProviderType** - odjava dobavljača identiteta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-180">**IdentityProviderType** - the identity provider of the identity being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-181">**IdentityUniqueID** - odjava ID identiteta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-181">**IdentityUniqueID** - the identity ID being signed out</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-182">**SessionEndTime** - vreme kada je sesija događaja završena</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-182">**SessionEndTime** - the time when the event session ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-183">**SignOutUserAction** - ukazuje na to da je korisnik započeo radnju odjavljivanja</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-183">**SignOutUserAction** - Indicates the user initiates the sign out action</span></span>

### <a name="officeidentitysspipromptwin32"></a><span data-ttu-id="9765f-184">Office.Identity.SspiPromptWin32</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-184">Office.Identity.SspiPromptWin32</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-185">Prikuplja se kada Office prikaže korisniku Windows SSPI upit za prijavljivanje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-185">Collected when Office shows the user a Windows SSPI sign-in prompt.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-186">Pored tihog preuzimanja tokena, upiti za potvrdu identiteta određuju da li se korisnik nalazi u statusu neispravne potvrde identiteta, što bi značilo da je stanje klijenta van mreže.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-186">Along with silent token acquisitions, authentication prompts determine whether a user is in a broken authentication state, which results in an Offline Client state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-187">Neispravna potvrda identiteta može sprečiti preuzimanje licence i dovesti do potpuno neupotrebljivog klijenta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-187">Broken authentication may prevent license acquisition and result in a completely unusable client.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-188">Windows SSPI upiti se koriste za potvrdu identiteta sa sistemom Exchange (za sinhronizaciju e-pošte) kada korisnikovi Exchange resursi nisu podešeni za višestruke potvrde identiteta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-188">Windows SSPI prompts are used for authenticating with Exchange (for mail synchronizing) when the user's Exchange resource hasn't been setup for multi-factor authentication.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-189">Ovi događaji, zajedno sa događajima prostora Office.MATS, koriste se za sledeće svrhe:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-189">These events, along with the Office.MATS namespace events, are used for the following purposes:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-190">1\) Utvrđivanje da li klijent može uspešno da pribavi token potvrde identiteta ili se nalazi u neispravnom stanju potvrde identiteta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-190">1\) Identify whether clients can successfully obtain an authentication token or have entered a broken authentication state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-191">2\) Procenjivanje da li su promene koje su se desile u klijentu ili uslugama dovele do kritičnih regresija u korisničkom iskustvu potvrde identiteta i pouzdanosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-191">2\) Evaluate whether changes that have occurred on the client or services have resulted in critical regressions in the user's authentication experience and reliability</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-192">3\) Kada dođe do greške, ovi signali emituju bitne kodove grešaka odgovornih komponenata (kôd Office klijenta, biblioteke potvrde identiteta, upravne usluge) i mogu se koristiti za trijažu, dijagnozu i ublažavanje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-192">3\) When failures occur, these signals emit important failure codes from the responsible component (Office client code, authentication libraries, or authority services) which can be used for triage, diagnosis and mitigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-193">4\) Ovi signali napajaju razne spremnosti otpreme i nadgledanja ispravnosti koja šalju upozorenja da bi naši inženjeri mogli brzo da odreaguju i da smanje vreme ublažavanja kritičnih grešaka koje blokiraju korisnika.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-193">4\) These signals power various ship readiness and health monitors which fire alerts so our engineers can engage quickly and reduce the time to mitigation of critical user-blocking failures</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-194">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-194">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-195">**AllowSavedCreds** - da li je novi akreditiv stalan</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-195">**AllowSavedCreds** - whether the new credential is persisted</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-196">**AuthScheme** - šema koja se koristi za potvrdu identiteta</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-196">**AuthScheme** - the authentication scheme used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-197">**CredsSaved** - da li je novi akreditiv sačuvan.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-197">**CredsSaved** - whether the new credential is saved</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-198">**DocumentUrlHash** - šifrovani URL zahtevi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-198">**DocumentUrlHash** - the encrypted URL requesting</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-199">**EndTag** - oznaka gde je upit završen.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-199">**EndTag** - the tag where the prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-205">**PromptEndTime** - vreme kada je upit završen</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-205">**PromptEndTime** - the time when the prompt ended</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-206">**PromptFailedTag** - oznaka koja označava neuspešnost SSPI upita</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-206">**PromptFailedTag** - the tag that indicates SSPI prompt failure</span></span>

### <a name="officematsactionofficewin32-officematsactionofficewinrt"></a><span data-ttu-id="9765f-244">Office.MATS.actionofficewin32, Office.MATS.actionofficewinrt</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-244">Office.MATS.actionofficewin32, Office.MATS.actionofficewinrt</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-245">Sledeći opisi se odnose na događaje Win32 i WinRT (ime zavisi od platforme)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-245">The following description applies for both Win32 and WinRT events (the name depends on platform.)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-246">Microsoft Auth Telemetry System (MATS) se prikuplja kada Office pokuša da preuzme token potvrde identiteta, ili tiho ili putem upita.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-246">Microsoft Auth Telemetry System (MATS) is collected when Office attempts to acquire an authentication token, either silently or through prompting.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-247">Kada pokušaj preuzimanja ne uspe, šalju se i informacije o grešci.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-247">When acquisition attempts fail, error information is included.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-248">Ovi događaji pomažu korisnicima da izbegnu unošenje neispravne identifikacije tako što će:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-248">These events help our users avoid entering broken authentication states by:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-249">1\) Utvrditi da li klijent može uspešno da pribavi token potvrde identiteta ili se nalazi u neispravnom stanju potvrde identiteta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-249">1\) Identifying whether clients can successfully obtain an authentication token or have entered a broken authentication state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-250">2\) Proceniti da li su promene koje su se desile u klijentu ili uslugama dovele do kritičnih regresija u korisničkom iskustvu potvrde identiteta i pouzdanosti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-250">2\) Evaluate when changes occur on the client or services, whether they result in critical regressions in the user's authentication experience and reliability</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-251">3\) Kada dođe do greške, ovi signali emituju bitne kodove grešaka odgovornih komponenata (kôd Office klijenta, biblioteke potvrde identiteta, upravne usluge) i mogu se koristiti za trijažu, dijagnozu i ublažavanje.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-251">3\) When failures occur, these signals emit important failure codes from the responsible component (Office client code, authentication libraries, or authority services) which can be used for triage, diagnosis and mitigation</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-252">4\) Ovi signali napajaju razne spremnosti otpreme i nadgledanja ispravnosti koja šalju upozorenja da bi naši inženjeri mogli brzo da odreaguju i da smanje vreme ublažavanja kritičnih grešaka.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-252">4\) These signals power various ship readiness and health monitors which fire alerts so our engineers can engage quickly and reduce the time to mitigation of critical failures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-253">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-253">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-254">**Actiontype** - koja biblioteka potvrde identiteta se koristi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-254">**Actiontype** - Which authentication library is used</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-255">**Appaudience** - da li je aplikacija napravljena za internu ili spoljnu upotrebu</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-255">**Appaudience** - Is the app build for internal or external use</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-256">**Appforcedprompt** - da li aplikacija poništava keš i nameće pojavljivanje upita</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-256">**Appforcedprompt** - Did the app override cache and force a prompt to be shown</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-257">**Appname** - ime aplikacije koja potvrđuje identitet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-257">**Appname** - Name of the application doing authentication</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-258">**Appver** - verzija aplikacije koja potvrđuje identitet</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-258">**Appver** - Version of the application doing authentication</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-259">**Askedforcreds** - da li aplikacija traži od korisnika da unese akreditive za ovu radnju</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-259">**Askedforcreds** - Did the application ask the user to enter credentials for this action</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-260">**Authoutcome** - da li je pokušaj potvrde identiteta uspešan, neuspešan ili otkazan.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-260">**Authoutcome** - Did the authentication attempt succeed, fail, or was cancelled</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-261">**Blockingprompt** - da li aplikacija izbacuje upit koji zahteva interakciju korisnika</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-261">**Blockingprompt** - Did the application throw a prompt requiring user interaction</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-262">**Correlationid** - GUID koji se koristi za spajanje sa uslužnim podacima</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-262">**Correlationid** - GUID used for joining with services data</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-263">**Count** - broj događaja u slučaju agregacije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-263">**Count** - Count of events in cases of aggregation</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-343">**Starttime** - Vreme kada je pozvana akcija\*pokretanja MATS API</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-343">**Starttime** - Time at which the Start\*Action MATS API was called</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-344">**Tenantid** - GUID identifikacija zakupca kojoj autorizovani korisnika pripada (u slučajevima kada to nije ADAL).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-344">**Tenantid** - GUID identifying the tenant the authenticated user belongs to (in non-ADAL cases).</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-345">**Uploadid** - Jedinstveni GUID za ovaj događaj koji se koristi za uklanjanje duplikata</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-345">**Uploadid** - Unique GUID for this event, used for de-duping</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-347">**Wamtelemetrybatch** - Trenutno nekorišćeno.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-347">**Wamtelemetrybatch** - Currently unused.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9765f-348">U budućnosti će omogućiti WAM komponenti da odašilje dodatne informacije koje se tiču događaja potvrde identiteta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-348">In the future, allows the WAM component to dispatch additional information regarding the authentication event.</span></span>

### <a name="officetelemetryvolumetrackingdata"></a><span data-ttu-id="9765f-2363">Office.Telemetry.VolumeTrackingData</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2363">Office.Telemetry.VolumeTrackingData</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-2364">Događaj količinskog praćenja metrike za događaj telemetrije</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2364">Event volume tracking metrics for telemetry events</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9765f-2365">Prikupljaju se sledeća polja:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2365">The following fields are collected:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-2366">**EventThreshold** - Maksimalan broj instanci jednog događaja koje mogu biti poslate u vremenskom okviru</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2366">**EventThreshold** - The maximum number of instances of a single event that can be sent in a window of time.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-2367">**HighestEventCount** - Najveći broj instanci jednog događaja koje su poslate u vremenskom okviru</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2367">**HighestEventCount** - The highest number of instances of a single event sent this window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-2368">**HighestEventName** - Ime događaja sa najvećim brojem instanci u vremenskom okviru.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2368">**HighestEventName** - The name of the event with the highest number of instances in this window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-2369">**TimeWindowInSeconds** - Trajanje vremenskog okvira u sekundama.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2369">**TimeWindowInSeconds** - The duration of the window in seconds.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-2370">**TotalEvents** - Ukupan broj događaja koji su poslati tokom vremenskog okvira.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2370">**TotalEvents** - The total number of events sent during the window.</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-2371">**UniqueEvents** - Broj jedinstvenih događaja koji su poslati tokom vremenskog okvira.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2371">**UniqueEvents** - The number of unique events sent during a window.</span></span>

### <a name="officetelemetrywritepayloadstodisk"></a><span data-ttu-id="9765f-2372">Office.Telemetry.WritePayloadsToDisk</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2372">Office.Telemetry.WritePayloadsToDisk</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="9765f-2375">**DetachedDuration** - Odvojeno trajanje u mikrosekundama</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9765f-2375">**DetachedDuration** - Detached duration in microseconds</span></span>
